  declare ~tempo := 0.
  declare %_repetition_interval_time[4096] := (0)
  declare %_repetition_interval_time_humanization[4096] := (0)
  declare $i00
  declare ~new_tempo0
  declare $i0
  declare $ii0
  declare $iii0
  ~new_tempo0 := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000)) / 960.
  if((~new_tempo0 # 0.) or ($NI_CALLBACK_TYPE # $NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER))
    $ii0 := 0
    $iii0 := 0
    $i0 := 0
    while($i0 <= 0) 
      $ii0 := 0
      while($ii0 <= 7) 
        $iii0 := 0
        while($iii0 <= 511) 
          if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i0 * 32) + (($ii0 * 4) + $iii0)]]] = 6)
            %_repetition_interval_time[($i0 * 4096) + (($ii0 * 512) + $iii0)] := int((60000. / ~new_tempo0) * (4. / real(%_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i0 * 32) + (($ii0 * 4) + $iii0)])))
          end if
          inc($iii0)
        end while
        inc($ii0)
      end while
      inc($i0)
    end while
    ~tempo := ~new_tempo0
  end if

    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
    $modwheel3 := %modulation_positions[0]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($modwheel3 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31) .or. sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
    if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $i20 := $idx17000
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
        $category0 := %type_to_category[%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]]]
        $i2 := 0
        while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] # -1)
            set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2]]])
            if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
              set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
            else
              set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
            end if
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
          end if
          inc($i2)
        end while
        $i2 := 0
        while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
          if($i2 = $category0)
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
          else
            set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
          end if
          inc($i2)
        end while
        $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $category0
      end if
    end if
  end if

function set_background_animation
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "bg_ani_" & (($frame0 / 32) + 1))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_bg), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ($frame0 mod 32) - ((($frame0 mod 32) - (30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame0 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)))) .and. sh_right((30 + abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(($frame0 / 32) - 3) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))) - ($frame0 mod 32), 31)))
end function
function set_key_colors
  $i3 := 0
  while($i3 <= 127) 
    set_key_color($i3, $KEY_COLOR_WHITE)
    if(($i3 >= 55) and ($i3 <= 96))
      set_key_color($i3, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
    end if
    inc($i3)
  end while
end function
function keyswitches_color_keys
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_keyswitch_selection
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "          ")
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE, "          ")
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_keyswitch[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE, !_articulation_names[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_control_par(%swi_keyswitch_purge[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_keyswitch_purge_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    set_key_pressed(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_RED)
    if(%_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] = 1)
      set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_ORANGE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $selected_subarticulation := 0
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $idx1700 := $idx17000
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_humanization[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_humanize & " ms")
    if(%_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] >= 0)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_release & " ms")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      $btn_articulation_release := 0
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "")
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $btn_articulation_release := 1
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
      set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
      inc($i)
    end while
    $idx170 := $idx1700
    $exception_idx1 := $selected_subarticulation
    $idx17 := 0
    while($idx17 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
      if($idx17 # $exception_idx1)
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      end if
      inc($idx17)
    end while
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
    else
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)

    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if

function keyswitches_on_note
  $check_before0 := 0
  $changed0 := 0
  if(in_range($note16, $keyswitch_octave * 12, (($keyswitch_octave * 12) + 8) - 1))
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 7) 
      $check_before0 := %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i]
      %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] := %KEY_DOWN[($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i]
      if($check_before0 # %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i])
        $changed0 := 1
      end if
      $selected_keyswitch := $note16 - ($keyswitch_octave * 12)
      inc($i)
    end while
    if($changed0 = 1)
      $idx17000 := $idx170000
      call update_keyswitch_selection
    end if
  end if
end function

function update_selected_notes
  $pressed_key_idx := 0
  $i := 127
  while($i >= 0) 
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $input_acceptance_time))
      $inst := 0
      while($inst <= 0) 
        $idx16 := ($num_pressed_keys - 1) - $pressed_key_idx
        $num_pressed_notes0 := $num_pressed_keys
        $note_selection0 := %note_selections[$inst]
        $result8 := $result80
        call is_in_note_selection
        if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 1)
          %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 1
          $instrument_slot0 := $inst
          $note4 := $i
          $velocity1 := %key_velocity[$i]
          $timing_offset0 := %pressed_keys[$i] - $ENGINE_UPTIME
          $ks0 := $result80
          $i8 := $i80
          $articulation_event_id5 := $articulation_event_id50
          $set_articulation_event_id0 := $set_articulation_event_id00
          $next_free_idx00 := $next_free_idx000
          $idx180 := $idx1800
          $i40 := $i400
          $is_free00 := $is_free000
          $_ret000 := $_ret0000
          $result900 := $result9000
          $i500 := $i5000
          $reduced_note00 := $reduced_note000
          $string00 := $string000
          $is_free10 := $is_free100
          $_ret1500 := $_ret15000
          $result910 := $result9100
          call articulations_on_note
        else
          %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 0
          $instrument_slot1 := $inst
          $note5 := $i
          $ks1 := $result80
          $i9 := $articulation_event_id50
          $release_offset0 := $set_articulation_event_id00
          $_ret220 := $i400
          $result100 := $next_free_idx000
          $result101 := $idx1800
          $is_active00 := $is_free100
          $i60 := $result9000
          $i501 := $is_free000
          $result102 := $i80
          $result103 := $i5000
          $result110 := $reduced_note000
          $result104 := $string000
          call articulations_note_off
        end if
        inc($inst)
      end while
    else
      if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
        $inst := 0
        while($inst <= 0) 
          $idx16 := ($num_pressed_keys - 1) - $pressed_key_idx
          $num_pressed_notes0 := $num_pressed_keys
          $note_selection0 := %note_selections[$inst]
          $result8 := $string000
          call is_in_note_selection
          if($is_in_note_selection_boolean = 0)
            $instrument_slot1 := $inst
            $note5 := $i
            $ks1 := $string000
            $i9 := $reduced_note000
            $release_offset0 := $i5000
            $_ret220 := $i80
            $result100 := $is_free000
            $result101 := $result9000
            $is_active00 := $is_free100
            $i60 := $idx1800
            $i501 := $next_free_idx000
            $result102 := $i400
            $result103 := $set_articulation_event_id00

            $result104 := $result80
            call articulations_note_off
            %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] := 0
          end if
          inc($inst)
        end while
      end if
    end if
    if(%pressed_keys[$i] > 0)
      inc($pressed_key_idx)
    end if
    dec($i)
  end while
  $inst := 0
  while($inst <= 0) 
    %active_notes[$inst] := 0
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 127) 
      if(%_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($inst * 128) + $i] = 1)
        inc(%active_notes[$inst])
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
    inc($inst)
  end while
end function

function subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr

    set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id6], $parameter0, $value4, $index0)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id6] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id6], $parameter0, $value4, $index0)
    end if
  end if
end function

    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id15] # -1)

end function
function articulations_compute_level
  ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0 := 0.
  $fade_in_start0 := %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch3 * 4) + $subarticulation2)]
  $fade_in_range0 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch3 * 4) + $subarticulation2)]
  $fade_out_end0 := %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch3 * 4) + $subarticulation2)]
  $fade_out_range0 := %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($instrument_slot2 * 32) + (($keyswitch3 * 4) + $subarticulation2)]
  if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start0, $fade_out_end0))
    ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0 := 1.
    if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_in_start0, $fade_in_start0 + $fade_in_range0) and ($fade_in_range0 > 0))
      ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0 := real(%modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation] - $fade_in_start0) / real($fade_in_range0)
    else
      if(in_range(%modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation], $fade_out_end0 - $fade_out_range0, $fade_out_end0) and ($fade_out_range0 > 0))
        ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0 := real($fade_out_end0 - %modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / real($fade_out_range0)
      end if
    end if
  end if
  $ret9 := int(1000000. * ((real(int(round(real(%_articulation_volume_min[($instrument_slot2 * 8) + $keyswitch3]) + (real(%_articulation_volume_max[($instrument_slot2 * 8) + $keyswitch3] - %_articulation_volume_min[($instrument_slot2 * 8) + $keyswitch3]) * pow(real(%modulation_positions[$note6 * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / 127., (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($instrument_slot2 * 8) + $keyswitch3]) / 100.) + 1.))))) / 127.) * ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0))
end function
function subarticulation_set_level
  $subarticulation_event_id6 := $subarticulation_event_id16
  $parameter0 := $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID
  $value4 := $level1
  $index0 := 2
  call subarticulation_event_set_event_par_arr
  if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id16] # -1)
    set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id16], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $level1, 2)
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id16] # -1)
      set_event_par_arr(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id16], $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $level1, 2)
    end if
  end if
  %subarticulation_event_level[$subarticulation_event_id16] := $level1
end function
function cc_on_controller
  $i10 := 0
  $_iter30 := 0
  $_iter20 := 0
  $_iter10 := 0
  while($_iter10 <= 0) 
    $_iter20 := 0
    while($_iter20 <= 7) 
      $_iter30 := 0
      while($_iter30 <= 127) 
        if(%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)] >= 0)
          $i10 := 0
          while($i10 <= 3) 
            $articulation_event_id0 := %_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]
            $subarticulation0 := $i10
            $result11 := $result111
            call articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id
            if($_ret300 >= 0)
              $articulation_event_id0 := %_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]
              $subarticulation0 := $i10
              $result11 := $result112
              call articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id
              $subarticulation_id3 := %subarticulation_event_subarticulation[$result111]
              $result13 := $result130
              call subarticulation_reacts_to_modwheel
              if($result112 = 1)
                $articulation_event_id0 := %_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]
                $subarticulation0 := $i10
                $result11 := $result113
                call articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id
                $subarticulation_event_id15 := $result130
                $modulation1 := int((1000000. * (real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[(%articulation_event_instrument[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 32) + ((%articulation_event_keyswitch[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 4) + $i10)]) + ((real(%modulation_positions[%articulation_event_note[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * $use_polyphonic_modulation]) / 127.) * real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[(%articulation_event_instrument[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 32) + ((%articulation_event_keyswitch[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 4) + $i10)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[(%articulation_event_instrument[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 32) + ((%articulation_event_keyswitch[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]] * 4) + $i10)])))) / 127.)
                call subarticulation_set_modulation
                $articulation_event_id0 := %_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]
                $subarticulation0 := $i10
                $result11 := $result113
                call articulation_event_get_subarticulation_event_id
                $ret9 := $result113
                $instrument_slot2 := %articulation_event_instrument[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]]
                $keyswitch3 := %articulation_event_keyswitch[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]]
                $note6 := %articulation_event_note[%_event_list[($_iter10 * 1024) + (($_iter20 * 128) + $_iter30)]]
                $subarticulation2 := $i10
                ~subarticulation_modulation_strength0 := ~subarticulation_modulation_strength00
                $fade_in_start0 := $fade_in_start00
                $fade_in_range0 := $fade_in_range00
                $fade_out_end0 := $fade_out_end00
                $fade_out_range0 := $fade_out_range00
                call articulations_compute_level
                $subarticulation_event_id16 := $result130
                $level1 := $result113
                call subarticulation_set_level
              end if
            end if
            inc($i10)
          end while
        end if
        inc($_iter30)
      end while
      inc($_iter20)
    end while
    inc($_iter10)
  end while
end function
function get_next_rr
  $rr1 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] = 0)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)] = 0)
      $rr1 := (%_rr_data_idx[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]]
    else
      $rr1 := random(0, %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - 1)
    end if
  else
    if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %_rr_data_time[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))]) > %subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]])
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)] = 0)
        $rr1 := (%_rr_data_idx[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]]
      else
        $rr1 := random(0, %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - 1)
      end if
    else
      if(%_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)] = 0)
        $rr1 := %subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - ((%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]])) .and. sh_right(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - ((%_rr_data_idx[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] + 1) mod %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]]), 31))
      else
        $rr1 := random(%subarticulations_rrr[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]], %subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($instrument5 * 32) + (($keyswitch9 * 4) + $subarticulation_idx3)]]] - 1)
      end if
    end if
    %_rr_data_time[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  end if
  %_rr_data_idx[($instrument5 * 4096) + (($keyswitch9 * 512) + (($subarticulation_idx3 * 128) + $note14))] := $rr1
end function
function subarticulation_event_get_free_index
  $result14 := -1
  $idx22 := 0
  while($idx22 < 128) 
    if((%subarticulation_event_list[$idx22] = -1) and (%subarticulation_event_last_used[$idx22] < ($ENGINE_UPTIME - $lookahead)))
      $result14 := $idx22
      $idx22 := 128
    end if
    $idx22 := $idx22 + 1
  end while
end function
function subarticulation_event_set_event_id
  %subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id0] := $event_id0
end function
function subarticulation_event_fade_out
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id12] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    fade_out(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id12], $fade_time0 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id12] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id12], $fade_time0 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id12] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id12], $fade_time0 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id12] # -1)
      fade_out(%subarticulation_event_transition_octave_event_id[$subarticulation_event_id12], $fade_time0 * 1000, $stop_voice0)
    end if
    if($stop_voice0 = 1)
      $subarticulation_event_id0 := $subarticulation_event_id12
      $event_id0 := -1
      call subarticulation_event_set_event_id
    end if
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_octave_layer_set_event_id
  %subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id1] := $event_id1
end function
function subarticulation_event_set_event_mark

    set_event_mark(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id9], $mark0)
    if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id9] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
      set_event_mark(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id9], $mark0)
    end if
  end if
end function

function repetition_engine_add

  if($idx23 # -1)
    %repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[$idx23] := $subarticulation_event0
    $repetition_engine_active := 1
    if($repetition_engine_start_time = -1)
      $repetition_engine_start_time := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    end if
  else
    message("REACHED MAX_SUBARTICULATIONS_IN_REPETITION_ENGINE")
  end if
end function
function update_authoring_labels
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " + " & $sli_sustain_release_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_start), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_trans_start & " + " & $sli_trans_start_offset & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 750.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " + " & (round((real($sli_trans_volume_offset) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " dB")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_fadeOut), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " + " & int((real($sli_trans_fadeOut_offset) / 1000000.) * 1000.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_wait), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_wait) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_wait_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " + " & int((real($sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset) / 1000000.) * 500.) & " ms")
end function

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_fadeIn), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note0 * 25) + (abs($end_note0 - $start_note0) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note0 - $start_note0), 31) * 12)))])

      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_start_offset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($start_note0 * 25) + (abs($end_note0 - $start_note0) + (- sh_right(- ($end_note0 - $start_note0), 31) * 12)))])

function last_transitions_update
  $i11 := 0
  while($i11 <= (num_elements(%_last_transitions) - 1)) 
    if(%_last_transitions[$i11] # -1)
      if(%_last_transitions_timecode[$i11] < ($ENGINE_UPTIME - 2000))
        %_last_transitions[$i11] := -1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i11)
  end while
end function
function last_transitions_contains
  $result15 := 0
  $i11 := $i110
  call last_transitions_update
  $i12 := 0
  while($i12 <= 7) 
    if(%_last_transitions[($instrument3 * 256) + (($keyswitch2 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx2 * 8) + $i12))] = ((128 * $transition_type1) + $note3))
      $result15 := 1
      %_last_transitions[($instrument3 * 256) + (($keyswitch2 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx2 * 8) + $i12))] := -1
    end if
    inc($i12)
  end while
end function
function last_transitions_add_event
  $idx24 := -1
  $min3 := %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + ($subarticulation_idx1 * 8))]
  $min_idx0 := 0
  $i13 := 0
  if($transition_type0 >= 0)
    $i13 := 0
    while($i13 <= 7) 
      if(%_last_transitions[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $i13))] = -1)
        $idx24 := $i13
        if($min3 > %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $i13))])
          $min3 := %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $i13))]
          $min_idx0 := $i13
        end if
      end if
      inc($i13)
    end while
    if($idx24 # -1)
      %_last_transitions[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $idx24))] := (128 * $transition_type0) + $note2
      %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $idx24))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    else
      %_last_transitions[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $min_idx0))] := (128 * $transition_type0) + $note2
      %_last_transitions_timecode[($instrument2 * 256) + (($keyswitch1 * 32) + (($subarticulation_idx1 * 8) + $min_idx0))] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    end if
  end if
end function
function repetition_engine_remove
  $idx25 := search(%repetition_engine_subarticulation_events, $subarticulation_event1)
  if($idx25 # -1)
    %repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[$idx25] := -1
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_note_off
  if(abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id14] - -1) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31)) = 1)
    $subarticulation_id4 := %subarticulation_event_subarticulation[$subarticulation_event_id14]
    $subarticulation_event1 := $subarticulation_event_id14
    $idx25 := $idx250
    call repetition_engine_remove
    if((%subarticulations_release_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id4]] = 0) or (($ENGINE_UPTIME - %last_pressed[%subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id14]]) < %subarticulations_release_time[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id4]]))
      $idx250 := %_articulation_release[(%articulation_event_instrument[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$subarticulation_event_id14]] * 8) + %articulation_event_keyswitch[%subarticulation_event_articulation_event[$subarticulation_event_id14]]]
      if($idx250 >= 0)
        $subarticulation_event_id12 := $subarticulation_event_id14
        $fade_time0 := $idx250
        $stop_voice0 := 1
        call subarticulation_event_fade_out
      else
        if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id4]] = 2)
          $idx250 := 300
          $subarticulation_event_id12 := $subarticulation_event_id14
          $fade_time0 := 300
          $stop_voice0 := 1
          call subarticulation_event_fade_out
        else
          note_off(%subarticulation_event_list[$subarticulation_event_id14])
          if(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id14] # -1)
            note_off(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer_id[$subarticulation_event_id14])
          end if
        end if
      end if
      if((%subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id4]] = 1) and (($authoring_page_active = 0) or ($btn_play_sustain = 1)))
        $event1 := play_note(%subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id14], %key_velocity[%subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id14]], 0, 0)
        $octave_event0 := -1
        if(%subarticulation_event_octave_layer[$subarticulation_event_id14] # 0)
          $octave_event0 := play_note(%subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id14] + 12, %key_velocity[%subarticulation_event_note[$subarticulation_event_id14]], 0, 0)
        end if

        end while

end function

              call articulation_event_is_event_active
              if($rr10 = 0)
                if(%delay_buffer[$i16] = %_last_articulation_event[(%delay_buffer_instrument[$i16] * 1024) + ((%delay_buffer_keyswitch[$i16] * 128) + %delay_buffer_note[$i16])])
                  %_last_articulation_event[(%delay_buffer_instrument[$i16] * 1024) + ((%delay_buffer_keyswitch[$i16] * 128) + %delay_buffer_note[$i16])] := -1
                end if
              end if
            end if
          end if
          %delay_buffer[$i16] := -1
        end if
        $all_inactive0 := 0
      end if
      inc($i16)
    end while
    if($all_inactive0 = 1)
      $any_delay_event_queued := 0
    end if
  end if
end function
function repetition_engine_update_tempo
  ~new_tempo0 := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000)) / 960.
  if((~new_tempo0 # ~tempo) or ($NI_CALLBACK_TYPE # $NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER))
    $ii0 := 0
    $iii0 := 0
    $i0 := 0
    while($i0 <= 0) 
      $ii0 := 0
      while($ii0 <= 7) 
        $iii0 := 0
        while($iii0 <= 511) 
          if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i0 * 32) + (($ii0 * 4) + $iii0)]]] = 6)
            %_repetition_interval_time[($i0 * 4096) + (($ii0 * 512) + $iii0)] := int((60000. / ~new_tempo0) * (4. / real(%_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i0 * 32) + (($ii0 * 4) + $iii0)])))
          end if
          inc($iii0)
        end while
        inc($ii0)
      end while
      inc($i0)
    end while
    ~tempo := ~new_tempo0
  end if
end function

            $any_event_played0 := 1

        inc($i)

function update_dynamic_range_cursor
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($modwheel3 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31) .or. sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function

end function

end function

  $modwheel2 := $modwheel4
  call update_circle_modwheel_position

end function
function subarticulation_group_count
  $group_count0 := 0
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] = 2)
    $group_count0 := 6 * ((%subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] * 3) + %subarticulations_trans_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]])
  else
    $group_count0 := (6 * %subarticulations_interval_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]) * ((%subarticulations_rr_num[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]] * %subarticulations_dynamic_layers[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]) * (1 + %subarticulations_release_group[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id0]]))
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_browser_load_category
  $i2 := 0
  while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] # -1)
      set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2]]])
      if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      end if
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
    inc($i2)
  end while
  $i2 := 0
  while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
    if($i2 = $category0)
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    end if
    inc($i2)
  end while
  $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $category0
end function
function move_legato_buffer_to_instrument
  $note_idx0 := 0
  $transition_idx0 := 0
  $dyn_layer_idx0 := 0
  while($dyn_layer_idx0 <= 1) 
    $note_idx0 := 0
    while($note_idx0 <= 127) 
      $transition_idx0 := 0
      while($transition_idx0 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]
        %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($instrument7 * 204800) + (($keyswitch11 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx5 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0))))] := %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx0 * 3200) + (($note_idx0 * 25) + $transition_idx0)]

function editor_page_open
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_humanization[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_humanize), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_humanize & " ms")
  if(%_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] >= 0)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_release[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_articulation_release & " ms")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    $btn_articulation_release := 0
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_articulation_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_articulation_release_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $btn_articulation_release := 1
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $idx170 := $idx1700
  $exception_idx1 := $selected_subarticulation
  $idx17 := 0
  while($idx17 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
    if($idx17 # $exception_idx1)
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    end if
    inc($idx17)
  end while
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)

    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")

  $i := 0

    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $modwheel3 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($modwheel3 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31) .or. sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
