function find_loaded_legato
  $authoring_page_active := 0
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[0] # -1)
    if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] = 2)
      $authoring_page_active := 1
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_authoring_legato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[0]]] & " (" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0] & ")")
    end if
  end if
end function
function authoring_open
  call find_loaded_legato
  $start_note0 := 60
  $end_note0 := 60
  $dynamic_layer0 := 0
  call update_authoring_transition
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_authoring), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function
function update_subarticulation_selection
  $exception_idx1 := $selected_subarticulation
  $idx17 := 0
  while($idx17 <= (num_elements(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection) - 1)) 
    if($idx17 # $exception_idx1)
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
    else
      set_control_par(%btn_edit_subarticulation_selection[$idx17], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    end if
    inc($idx17)
  end while
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    " & !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]])
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "    Empty")
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_solo_subarticulation), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_subarticulations_solo_states[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_volume & " dB")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 0) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 5)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_tightness & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_tightness_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode := %_loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_rr_mode), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_rr_mode_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 6)
    $mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed := %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_subarticulation_repetition_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_repetition_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(((%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 1) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)) or (%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 4))
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_vibrato & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_vibrato_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  end if
  if(%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]] = 2)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_volume & " dB")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_volume_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed & " %")
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_subarticulation_trans_speed_title), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed := %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  end if
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $modwheel3 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($modwheel3 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31) .or. sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function subarticulation_browser_open
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] # -1)
    $category0 := %type_to_category[%subarticulations_type[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]]]]
    $i2 := 0
    while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection) - 1)) 
      set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] # -1)
        set_control_par_str(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !subarticulations_full_name[%subarticulations_ids_positions[%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2]]])
        if(%_subarticulation_browser_entries[($category0 * 14) + $i2] = %_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)])
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
        else
          set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
        end if
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_selection[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      end if
      inc($i2)
    end while
    $i2 := 0
    while($i2 <= (num_elements(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category) - 1)) 
      if($i2 = $category0)
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
      else
        set_control_par(%btn_subarticulation_browser_category[$i2], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
      end if
      inc($i2)
    end while
    $subarticulation_browser_active_category := $category0
  end if
end function
function subarticulation_browser_close
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_subarticulation_browser), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_title), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
end function
function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_keyswitch_volume_curve), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch] * -1)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, int(round(real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) + (real(int((real(%_articulation_volume_max[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.) - int((real(%_articulation_volume_min[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 127.) * 30.)) * pow(real($i) / real(num_elements(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope)), (real(%_articulation_volume_curve[($selected_instrument * 8) + $selected_keyswitch]) / 100.) + 1.)))))
    set_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - get_control_par(%lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_control
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(-200. + ((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_in), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH)))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_constant), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_fade_out), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 200.))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_modwheel_assignment_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
end function
function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 3) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)] # -1)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      if($i = $selected_subarticulation)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & $i)
      else
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & $i)
        set_control_par_str(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & $i)
      end if
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_left[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
      set_control_par(%lbl_center_circle_bound_right[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, 127 - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $i)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update_dynamic_range_control
  ?xy_dynamic_range[0] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  ?xy_dynamic_range[2] := real(%_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) / 127.
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_dynamic_range[2] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line_inactive), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_line), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  $modwheel3 := %modulation_positions[0]
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_cursor), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 5) + int((real((($modwheel3 * (1 + (sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31) .or. sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)))) - sh_right($modwheel3 - 1, 31)) - (127 * sh_right(127 - $modwheel3, 31))) / 127.) * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_right), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_dynamic_range_bound_left), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))))
end function
function center_circle_distance
  ~dx0 := ~x17 - 0.5
  ~dy0 := ~y3 - 0.5
  ~ret15 := sqrt((~dx0 * ~dx0) + (~dy0 * ~dy0))
end function
function center_circle_angle
  ~dx1 := ~x18 - 0.5
  ~dy1 := ~y4 - 0.5
  ~cos_theta0 := ~dx1 / sqrt((~dx1 * ~dx1) + (~dy1 * ~dy1))
  ~angle1 := acos(~cos_theta0)
  if(~dy1 < 0.)
    ~angle1 := (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI) - ~angle1
  end if
end function
function angle_to_value
  ~new_angle0 := ~angle0 + (~NI_MATH_PI / 2.)
  if(~new_angle0 > (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.))
    ~new_angle0 := ~new_angle0 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI)
  end if
  ~new_angle0 := abs(~new_angle0 - (2. * ~NI_MATH_PI))
  $ret17 := int((127. * (~new_angle0 - ~angle_min0)) / (~angle_max0 - ~angle_min0))
end function
function move_to_legato_buffer
  $note_idx1 := 0
  $transition_idx1 := 0
  $dyn_layer_idx1 := 0
  while($dyn_layer_idx1 <= 1) 
    $note_idx1 := 0
    while($note_idx1 <= 127) 
      $transition_idx1 := 0
      while($transition_idx1 <= 24) 
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_wait_time[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_start[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_sus_wait_time_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_in_time_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_fade_out_time_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_start_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        %_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset[($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1)] := %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($instrument8 * 204800) + (($keyswitch12 * 25600) + (($subarticulation_idx6 * 6400) + (($dyn_layer_idx1 * 3200) + (($note_idx1 * 25) + $transition_idx1))))]
        inc($transition_idx1)
      end while
      inc($note_idx1)
    end while
    inc($dyn_layer_idx1)
  end while
end function
on persistence_changed
  $frame0 := %CC[1]
  call set_background_animation
  call set_key_colors
  call keyswitches_color_keys
end on
on note
  ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 1)
  $note16 := $EVENT_NOTE
  call keyswitches_on_note
  if(%pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] = -1)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %last_pressed[$EVENT_NOTE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
    %key_velocity[$EVENT_NOTE] := $EVENT_VELOCITY
    inc($num_pressed_keys)
  end if
  $last_on_note_callback := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  $wait_time0 := $note_selection_time * 1000
  call wait_or_zero
  if($last_on_note_callback = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_selected_notes
  end if
end on
on release
  if(get_event_mark($EVENT_ID, $MARK_1) = 0)
    set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 0)
    $last_release_callback := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
    ignore_event($EVENT_ID)
    %pressed_keys[$EVENT_NOTE] := -1
    dec($num_pressed_keys)
    if($sustain_pedal = 0)
      $instrument_slot1 := 0
      $note5 := $EVENT_NOTE
      call articulations_note_off
      $wait_time0 := $note_selection_time * 1000
      call wait_or_zero
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 0) 
        %_pressed_notes_per_instrument[($i * 128) + $EVENT_NOTE] := 0
        inc($i)
      end while
      if($last_release_callback = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
        call update_selected_notes
      end if
    end if
  end if
end on
on controller
  ignore_controller
  %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] := %CC[$CC_NUM]
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $frame1 := %CC[1]
    call buffer_modwheel_animation
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_modwheel_slider), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %CC[1])
  end if
  if($CC_NUM = 64)
    if(%CC[64] > 63)
      $sustain_pedal_actual := 1
    else
      $sustain_pedal_actual := 0
      $sustain_pedal := 0
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 127) 
        if(%pressed_keys[$i] = -1)
          $ii := 0
          while($ii <= 0) 
            $instrument_slot1 := $ii
            $note5 := $i
            call articulations_note_off
            inc($ii)
          end while
        end if
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
  end if
  $wait_time0 := ($lookahead * 1000) * $use_constant_delay
  call wait_or_zero
  $sustain_pedal := $sustain_pedal_actual
  if($CC_NUM = 1)
    $note13 := 0
    $value5 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    call set_modulation_position
    call cc_on_controller
  end if
end on
on poly_at
  $note13 := $POLY_AT_NUM
  $value5 := %POLY_AT[$POLY_AT_NUM]
  call set_modulation_position
  call cc_on_controller
end on
on listener
  call delay_buffer_execute
  call repetition_engine_listener
  if(($animation_frame_counter = 0) and ($next_modwheel_animation_frame # -1))
    $frame0 := $next_modwheel_animation_frame
    call set_background_animation
    if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($pnl_editor_page), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
      $modwheel4 := $next_modwheel_animation_frame
      call editor_update_modwheel_position
    end if
    $next_modwheel_animation_frame := -1
  end if
  $animation_frame_counter := ($animation_frame_counter + 1) mod 4
end on
on ui_controls
  $uiid1 := $NI_UI_ID
  $idx26 := search(%swi_keyswitch, $NI_UI_ID)
  if($idx26 # -1)
    if(get_control_par(%swi_keyswitch[$idx26], $CONTROL_PAR_KEY_SHIFT) = 0)
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 7) 
        %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $i] := 0
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
    %_keyswitch_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $idx26] := 1
    $selected_keyswitch := $idx26
    $idx17000 := $idx170001
    call update_keyswitch_selection
  end if
  $idx26 := search(%swi_keyswitch_purge, $uiid1)
  if($idx26 # -1)
    %_keyswitch_purge_states[($selected_instrument * 8) + $idx26] := get_control_par(%swi_keyswitch_purge[$idx26], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    $_ret6600 := $_ret66000
    $group_count000 := $group_count0000
    $group_count001 := $group_count0010
    $i17 := 0
    $ii4 := 0
    $iii1 := 0
    $_iter0 := 0
    while($_iter0 <= (num_elements(%subarticulation_is_loaded0) - 1)) 
      %subarticulation_is_loaded0[$_iter0] := 0
      inc($_iter0)
    end while
    $i17 := 0
    while($i17 <= 0) 
      $ii4 := 0
      while($ii4 <= 7) 
        $iii1 := 0
        while($iii1 <= 3) 
          if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)] # -1)
            %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] := %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] + %_keyswitch_purge_states[($i17 * 8) + $ii4]
          end if
          inc($iii1)
        end while
        inc($ii4)
      end while
      inc($i17)
    end while
    $i17 := 0
    while($i17 <= 511) 
      if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$i17] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
        if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$i17] = 0)
          $subarticulation_id1 := $i17
          $purge_state0 := 0
          $_ret660 := $_ret6600
          $group_count00 := $group_count000
          $i17 := 0
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $group_count00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          while($i17 <= ($_ret660 - 1))

on ui_control(?xy_modwheel_assignment)
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[1] := 1.
  ?xy_modwheel_assignment[5] := 1.
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) or (get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    end if
  else
    if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    end if
  end if
  $ma_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 2) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
    if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] < ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2])
      ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]
    end if
    %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] * 127.)
  else
    if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 0) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[0])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[2] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]))
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
      %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(round((?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[2]) * 127.))
    else
      if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 4) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4])) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fade_circle_md), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH) - 20)))
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int((?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] - ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4]) * 127.)
      else
        if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(?xy_modwheel_assignment), $CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX) = 6) and (?xy_modwheel_assignment[0] <= ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]))
          if(?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] > ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6])
            ?xy_modwheel_assignment[4] := ?xy_modwheel_assignment[6]
          end if
          %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := int(?xy_modwheel_assignment[6] * 127.)
        end if
      end if
    end if
  end if
  wait(10000)
  if($ma_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID)
    call update_modwheel_assignment_control
    call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
  end if
end on

  end if

  %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := $sli_subarticulation_trans_speed
end on
on ui_control($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed)
  %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := $btn_subarticulation_trans_speed
  if($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed = 1)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  else
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_subarticulation_trans_speed_blocker), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  end if
end on
on ui_control(?xy_center_circles)
  $cc_cb_id := $NI_CALLBACK_ID
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN)
    ~ret15 := ?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~x17 := ?xy_center_circles[0]
    ~y3 := ?xy_center_circles[1]
    call center_circle_distance
    ~x18 := ?xy_center_circles[0]
    ~y4 := ?xy_center_circles[1]
    call center_circle_angle
    $ret17 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~angle0 := ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
    ~angle_min0 := 0.7
    ~angle_max0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
    call angle_to_value
    if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.32) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.36))
      $selected_subarticulation := 0
    else
      if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.36) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.4))
        $selected_subarticulation := 1
      else
        if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.4) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.44))
          $selected_subarticulation := 2
        else
          if((?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] >= 0.44) and (?distance0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < 0.48))
            $selected_subarticulation := 3
          end if
        end if
      end if
    end if
    if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
      $selected_circle_end := 0
    else
      if(abs(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] - %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) < 10)
        $selected_circle_end := 1
      else
        $selected_circle_end := -1
      end if
    end if
    call update_subarticulation_selection
  end if
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG)
    wait(10000)
    if(($cc_cb_id = $NI_CALLBACK_ID) and ($selected_circle_end # -1))
      ~x18 := ?xy_center_circles[0]
      ~y4 := ?xy_center_circles[1]
      call center_circle_angle
      $ret17 := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
      ~angle0 := ?angle2[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
      ~angle_min0 := 0.7
      ~angle_max0 := (~NI_MATH_PI * 2.) - 0.7
      call angle_to_value
      if($selected_circle_end = 0)
        if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] < ((%_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) - %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
          %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
        end if
      else
        if($selected_circle_end = 1)
          if(%controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100] > ((%_loaded_subarticulations_start[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]) + %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)]))
            %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($selected_instrument * 32) + (($selected_keyswitch * 4) + $selected_subarticulation)] := %controller_value0[$NI_CALLBACK_ID mod 100]
          end if
        end if
      end if
      call update_modwheel_assignment_control
      call update_modwheel_assignment_circles
    end if
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
  $uiid0 := %btn_mixer_channel_enable[4]
  $idx27 := search(%sli_mixer_channel_volume, $uiid0)
  if($idx27 # -1)
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, get_control_par(%sli_mixer_channel_volume[$idx27], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE), -1, -1, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + $idx27)
    if($idx27 = 4)
      set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, get_control_par(%sli_mixer_channel_volume[$idx27], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE), -1, -1, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + 5)
    end if
  end if
  $idx27 := search(%btn_mixer_channel_enable, $uiid0)
  if($idx27 # -1)
    if($idx27 < 4)
      %microphone_position_states[$idx27] := get_control_par(%btn_mixer_channel_enable[$idx27], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    else
      %microphone_position_states[$idx27 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel] := get_control_par(%btn_mixer_channel_enable[$idx27], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
      %microphone_position_states[$idx27 + (1 - $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)] := 0
    end if
    $_ret6600 := $_ret66001
    $group_count000 := $group_count0001
    $group_count001 := $group_count0011
    $i17 := 0
    $ii4 := 0
    $iii1 := 0
    $_iter0 := 0
    while($_iter0 <= (num_elements(%subarticulation_is_loaded0) - 1)) 
      %subarticulation_is_loaded0[$_iter0] := 0
      inc($_iter0)
    end while
    $i17 := 0
    while($i17 <= 0) 
      $ii4 := 0
      while($ii4 <= 7) 
        $iii1 := 0
        while($iii1 <= 3) 
          if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)] # -1)
            %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] := %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] + %_keyswitch_purge_states[($i17 * 8) + $ii4]
          end if
          inc($iii1)
        end while
        inc($ii4)
      end while
      inc($i17)
    end while
    $i17 := 0
    while($i17 <= 511) 
      if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$i17] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
        if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$i17] = 0)
          $subarticulation_id1 := $i17
          $purge_state0 := 0
          $_ret660 := $_ret6600
          $group_count00 := $group_count000
          $i17 := 0
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $group_count00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          while($i17 <= ($_ret660 - 1)) 
            purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i17) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i17 mod 6])
            inc($i17)
            $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
            $group_count0 := $group_count00
            call subarticulation_group_count
          end while
        end if
      end if
      inc($i17)
    end while
    $i17 := 0
    while($i17 <= 511) 
      if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$i17] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
        if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$i17] > 0)
          $subarticulation_id1 := $i17
          $purge_state0 := 1
          $_ret660 := $group_count000
          $group_count00 := $group_count001
          $i17 := 0
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $group_count00
          call subarticulation_group_count
          while($i17 <= ($_ret660 - 1)) 
            purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i17) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i17 mod 6])
            inc($i17)
            $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
            $group_count0 := $group_count00
            call subarticulation_group_count
          end while
        end if
      end if
      inc($i17)
    end while
  end if
  attach_level_meter(%lvl_mixer_channel_volume[8], -1, -1, 0, 4 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
  attach_level_meter(%lvl_mixer_channel_volume[9], -1, -1, 1, 4 + $mnu_mixer_bleed_channel)
end on
on ui_control($btn_unpurge_all)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%microphone_position_states) - 1)) 
    %microphone_position_states[$i] := 1
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i17 := 0
  $ii4 := 0
  $iii1 := 0
  $_iter0 := 0
  while($_iter0 <= (num_elements(%subarticulation_is_loaded0) - 1)) 
    %subarticulation_is_loaded0[$_iter0] := 0
    inc($_iter0)
  end while
  $i17 := 0
  while($i17 <= 0) 
    $ii4 := 0
    while($ii4 <= 7) 
      $iii1 := 0
      while($iii1 <= 3) 
        if(%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)] # -1)
          %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] := %subarticulation_is_loaded0[%_loaded_subarticulations[($i17 * 32) + (($ii4 * 4) + $iii1)]] + %_keyswitch_purge_states[($i17 * 8) + $ii4]
        end if
        inc($iii1)
      end while
      inc($ii4)
    end while
    inc($i17)
  end while
  $i17 := 0
  while($i17 <= 511) 
    if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$i17] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
      if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$i17] = 0)
        $subarticulation_id1 := $i17
        $purge_state0 := 0
        $_ret660 := $_ret6600
        $group_count00 := $group_count000
        $i17 := 0
        $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
        $group_count0 := $group_count00
        call subarticulation_group_count
        while($i17 <= ($_ret660 - 1)) 
          purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i17) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i17 mod 6])
          inc($i17)
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $group_count00
          call subarticulation_group_count
        end while
      end if
    end if
    inc($i17)
  end while
  $i17 := 0
  while($i17 <= 511) 
    if(%subarticulations_group_idx[$i17] # $NI_NOT_FOUND)
      if(%subarticulation_is_loaded0[$i17] > 0)
        $subarticulation_id1 := $i17
        $purge_state0 := 1
        $_ret660 := $group_count000
        $group_count00 := $group_count001
        $i17 := 0
        $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
        $group_count0 := $group_count00
        call subarticulation_group_count
        while($i17 <= ($_ret660 - 1)) 
          purge_group((%subarticulations_group_idx[%subarticulations_ids_positions[$subarticulation_id1]] + $i17) + 1, $purge_state0 * %microphone_position_states[$i17 mod 6])
          inc($i17)
          $subarticulation_id0 := $subarticulation_id1
          $group_count0 := $group_count00
          call subarticulation_group_count
        end while
      end if
    end if
    inc($i17)
  end while
end on

  call subarticulation_browser_close
end on

on ui_control($mnu_settings_keyswitch_position)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 7) 
    set_key_pressed(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, %KEY_DOWN[($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i])
    set_key_color(($keyswitch_octave * 12) + $i, $KEY_COLOR_WHITE)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $keyswitch_octave := get_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_settings_keyswitch_position), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  call update_keyswitch_selection
end on
on ui_control($mnu_lookahead)
  $lookahead := $mnu_lookahead
end on
on ui_control($btn_factory_reset)
  $offset100 := 0
  $end_note200 := 0
  $i110000 := 0
  while($i110000 <= 0) 
    %octave_layer[$i110000] := 0
    %octave_shift[$i110000] := 0
    $offset100 := 0
    while($offset100 <= 7) 
      !_articulation_names[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := "Empty"
      %_articulation_volume_min[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_volume_max[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 127
      %_articulation_volume_curve[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_humanization[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := 0
      %_articulation_release[($i110000 * 8) + $offset100] := -1
      $end_note200 := 0
      while($end_note200 <= 3) 
        %_loaded_subarticulations[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := -1
        %_loaded_subarticulations_start[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_end[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 127
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_volume[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_tightness[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 127
        %_loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulations_trans_volume[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 0
        %_loaded_subarticulation_trans_speed_auto[($i110000 * 32) + (($offset100 * 4) + $end_note200)] := 1
        inc($end_note200)
      end while
      inc($offset100)
    end while
    inc($i110000)
  end while
end on
on ui_control($sli_sustain_release)
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_sus_release_time[$i] := $sli_sustain_release
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_sus_release_time[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_sustain_release
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " + " & $sli_sustain_release_offset & " ms")
end on
on ui_control($sli_sustain_release_offset)
  $sli_sustain_release_offset := (($sli_sustain_release_offset * (1 + (sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_release) - $sli_sustain_release_offset, 31) .or. sh_right($sli_sustain_release_offset - - $sli_sustain_release, 31)))) - (- $sli_sustain_release * sh_right($sli_sustain_release_offset - - $sli_sustain_release, 31))) - ((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_release) * sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_sustain_release) - $sli_sustain_release_offset, 31))
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[$i] := $sli_sustain_release_offset
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_sus_release_time_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_sustain_release_offset
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sustain_release), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $sli_sustain_release & " + " & $sli_sustain_release_offset & " ms")
end on

on ui_control($sli_trans_volume)
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[$i] := $sli_trans_volume
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_trans_volume
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " + " & (round((real($sli_trans_volume_offset) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " dB")
end on
on ui_control($sli_trans_volume_offset)
  $sli_trans_volume_offset := (($sli_trans_volume_offset * (1 + (sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_trans_volume) - $sli_trans_volume_offset, 31) .or. sh_right($sli_trans_volume_offset - - $sli_trans_volume, 31)))) - (- $sli_trans_volume * sh_right($sli_trans_volume_offset - - $sli_trans_volume, 31))) - ((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_trans_volume) * sh_right((get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_MAX_VALUE) - $sli_trans_volume) - $sli_trans_volume_offset, 31))
  if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_authoring_edit_all), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = 1)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= 6399) 
      %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[$i] := $sli_trans_volume_offset
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    %_legato_data_trans_zone_volume_offset[($mnu_authoring_dynamic_layer * 3200) + (($vlue_authoring_start_note * 25) + (abs($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note) + (- sh_right(- ($vlue_authoring_end_note - $vlue_authoring_start_note), 31) * 12)))] := $sli_trans_volume_offset
  end if
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_trans_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (round((real($sli_trans_volume) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " + " & (round((real($sli_trans_volume_offset) / 1000.) * pow(10., 2.)) / pow(10., 2.)) & " dB")
end on

on ui_control($btn_save_authoring)
  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    $instrument8 := 0
    $keyswitch12 := 0
    $subarticulation_idx6 := 0
    call move_to_legato_buffer
    @legato_name1 := "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0]
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_release_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_wait_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_wait.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_fade_in_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_release_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_wait_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_start_offset.nka")
    save_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name1 & "_sus_trans_zone_wait_offset.nka")
  else
    message("No Legato Loaded")
  end if
  $btn_save_authoring := 0
end on
on ui_control($btn_load_authoring)
  if($authoring_page_active = 1)
    @legato_name0 := "leg" & %_loaded_subarticulations[0]
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_fade_in_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_release_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_wait_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_zone_start.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_zone_volume.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_fade_in_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_release_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_release_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_sus_wait_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_wait_time.nka_offset"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_in_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_fade_in_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_fade_out_time_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_fade_out_time_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_start_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_zone_start_offset.nka"))
    wait_async(load_array_str(%_legato_data_buffer_trans_zone_volume_offset, @LEGATO_ARRAY_PATH & @legato_name0 & "_sus_trans_zone_volume_offset.nka"))
    $instrument7 := 0
    $keyswitch11 := 0
    $subarticulation_idx5 := 0
    call move_legato_buffer_to_instrument
    $start_note0 := 60
    $end_note0 := 60
    $dynamic_layer0 := 0
    call update_authoring_transition
  else
    message("No Legato Loaded")
  end if
  $btn_load_authoring := 0
end on
on ui_control($btn_credits_backdrop)
  call credits_close
end on
